### [1] [Applying Deep Learning for cockpit segmentation in the context of mixed reality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06520)
*Alexandre Leles Sousa,Pedro de Oliveira Nielson,Erick Oliveira Rodrigues,Rafael Francisco dos Santos,Giovani Bernardes Vitor*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究基于人工智能的图像分割技术，应用于矿用卡车模拟器CAT793F的实时图像处理，旨在实现虚拟与现实环境的无缝融合。通过使用U-Net和DeepLabV3+卷积神经网络进行图像分割，识别前景与背景，提升混合现实中的沉浸感。实验结果显示分割准确率接近90%，其中最优模型被成功确定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了提升混合现实中虚拟与真实图像融合的沉浸感，需要精确区分图像中的前景与背景，从而实现实时、自然的环境融合。传统方法难以满足高精度与实时性要求，因此引入深度学习技术以优化图像分割效果。

Method: 利用CAT793F矿用卡车模拟器采集真实场景图像，采用摄像头获取用户视角图像，并应用U-Net与DeepLabV3+两种卷积神经网络架构进行图像分割。通过训练与评估，对比不同模型在分割任务中的表现，最终选择最优模型。

Result: 实验结果表明，所提方法在图像分割任务中达到约90%的准确率，其中DeepLabV3+表现更优，成为最佳模型，有效支持了虚拟与现实图像的实时融合。

Conclusion: 本研究成功验证了基于深度学习的图像分割技术在混合现实应用中的有效性，特别是U-Net与DeepLabV3+在真实场景图像分割中表现出色，为未来增强现实与虚拟环境融合提供了可靠的技术支持。

Abstract: Computer vision is an area that has been growing continuously. With the advance of technologies with a first-person view, new development opportunities have emerged inside the area. Mixed reality promotes virtual environments with objects from the physical world shown in real time. For that, it's necessary to be concerned with the immersion of the user in this simulated environment, increasingly seeking to bring it closer to a possible desired reality. This paper proposes the development of image processing in order to perform the segmentation of images to identify what is foreground and background in order to facilitate the union of virtual and real images. Thus, the present work obtain real images of the user using the off-highway truck simulator CAT793F, through a camera, to be able to perform the segmentation of such images with artificial intelligence techniques.The convolutional neural network architectures "U-net" and "DeepLabV3+" are applied to perform image segmentation. As a result, metrics with around 90% accuracy were presented and and the best model was determined.

</details>


### [2] [GOPAgen: Motion-Aware and Efficient Agentic Long-Video Understanding with Structural Memory and Hierarchical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06532)
*Haozhe Chi,Yang Jin,Yadong Mu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: GOPAgen提出一种新方法，通过将视频编码器中的GOP（图像组）引入视频理解框架，结合运动代理、GOP树推理算法和结构化记忆机制，实现对视频局部细节运动的高效理解。同时引入运动矢量数据库支持多粒度检索，显著提升视频问答性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在视频理解中缺乏对详细运动的把握以及高效的内存架构，限制了对复杂动作的精准分析。

Method: 集成视频编码器中的GOP到理解框架；设计基于GOP的运动代理；提出GOP树推理算法；构建融合局部运动信息与详细描述的结构化记忆机制；开发粗到细的逐级深入算法；引入运动矢量数据库以支持高效检索。

Result: 在MotionBench和Egoschema等多个视频理解基准上取得优异的视频问答表现，验证了框架的有效性与优越性。

Conclusion: GOPAgen通过结合视频编码特性与结构化记忆机制，实现了对视频中局部运动的精细建模，显著提升了长视频理解能力。

Abstract: Despite significant progress in agentic long video understanding, existing methods still lack detailed motion comprehension coupled with an efficient memory architecture. In this paper, we propose GOPAgen, a novel approach that first integrates video codec into the video understanding framework via a meticulously designed motion agent trained on Groups of Pictures (GOPs) from video codec. We further develop a GOP tree reasoning algorithm, which is naturally aligned with video codec and enhances the model's ability to understand local detailed motions in videos. Additionally, we carefully design a structural memory mechanism that integrates local motion information with detailed captions in structural pages, and propose an efficient coarse-to-fine zoom-in algorithm to fully exploit the structural memory. Furthermore, we incorporate a motion vector database into the framework to enable efficient retrieval of motion vectors at different granularities. Overall, our method achieves superior Video Question Answering (VQA) performance on various video understanding benchmarks, including MotionBench and Egoschema, thereby demonstrating the superiority of our proposed framework.

</details>


### [3] [Attention-Guided Autoencoder Fusion for Insulator Defect Detection Using UAV Transmission-Line Imaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06536)
*Malak Allam,Khaled Shaban,Ali Hamdi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出AE-YOLO框架，结合注意力引导的自编码器与YOLO，解决高压输电线绝缘子缺陷检测中的类别不平衡、尺度变化大和缺陷空间范围小等问题。通过轻量级瓶颈自编码器保留异常敏感信息，引入CBAM模块增强特征区分度，采用方差最大化自编码器正则化策略提升缺陷判别性。训练使用联合损失函数（焦点损失、CIoU损失、自编码器正则化），推理阶段融合多个YOLO版本预测并引入置信度增强机制，显著提升对罕见缺陷类别的敏感性。在Insulator-Defect Detection数据集上，该方法实现95.10% mAP@0.5、96.40%精度和93.80%召回率，优于最强基线5.0点mAP和6.7点召回率，验证了其有效性与可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高电压输电线路绝缘子缺陷检测面临严重类别不平衡、尺度变化大以及缺陷在无人机影像中空间范围小等挑战，传统方法难以有效应对，亟需更鲁棒且高效的检测框架。

Method: 提出AE-YOLO框架，将轻量级瓶颈自编码器嵌入FPN-PAN结构中以保留异常敏感特征；在骨干网络中引入CBAM模块增强特征区分能力；设计方差最大化自编码器正则化策略以生成多样化的缺陷判别性表征；采用融合焦点损失、CIoU损失与自编码器正则化的统一目标函数进行训练；推理时利用WBF融合YOLOv8/v10/v11输出，并通过自编码器引导的置信度提升机制增强对稀有缺陷类别的检测灵敏度。

Result: 在Insulator-Defect Detection数据集上，基于EfficientNetV2主干网络的AE-YOLO模型达到95.10% mAP@0.5、96.40%精度和93.80%召回率，相较于最强YOLO基线提升5.0个百分点mAP@0.5和6.7个百分点召回率，表现出优越的检测性能与泛化能力。

Conclusion: AE-YOLO框架有效解决了无人机影像中绝缘子缺陷检测的关键难题，具备良好的鲁棒性、准确性和可扩展性，是一种适用于实际电力巡检场景的高效解决方案。

Abstract: Automated defect detection in high-voltage transmission-line insulators remains challenging due to severe class imbalance, large scale variation, and the small spatial extent of defect instances in Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV) imagery. To address these challenges, this paper proposes AE-YOLO, an Attention-Guided AutoEncoder-Enhanced YOLO framework for robust insulator defect detection. The architecture integrates lightweight bottleneck autoencoders within a Feature Pyramid Network-Path Aggregation Network (FPN-PAN) neck. This preserves anomaly-sensitive information during multi-scale feature fusion. Convolutional Block Attention Modules (CBAM) are used throughout the backbone, enhancing feature discrimination and suppressing background interference. The framework also introduces a variance-maximizing autoencoder regularization strategy, which encourages diverse, defect-discriminative latent representations. The network trains using a unified objective that combines focal loss, Complete IoU (CIoU) loss, and autoencoder regularization to address foreground-background imbalance and improve localization accuracy. During inference, Weighted Boxes Fusion (WBF) combines predictions from YOLOv8, YOLOv10, and YOLO11. An autoencoder-guided confidence boosting mechanism improves sensitivity to rare defect categories. Experiments on the Insulator-Defect Detection dataset show that AE-YOLO with an EfficientNetV2 backbone achieves 95.10 percent mAP at 0.5, 96.40 percent precision, and 93.80 percent recall. This performance surpasses the strongest YOLO-family baseline by 5.0 points in mAP at 0.5 and 6.7 points in recall. These results confirm the effectiveness and adaptability of the framework. The model is a practical and scalable solution for UAV-based transmission-line inspection and defect monitoring.

</details>


### [4] [WorldBench: A Challenging and Visually Diverse Multimodal Reasoning Benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06538)
*Yida Yin,Harish Krishnakumar,Chung Peng Lee,Boya Zeng,Wenhao Chai,Shengbang Tong,Wenhu Chen,Hu Xu,Xingyu Fu,Gabriel Sarch,Aleksandra Korolova,Zhuang Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出WorldBench，一个具有高度视觉多样性的多模态大模型推理基准，通过构建跨领域的视觉概念分类体系并采集丰富图像数据，设计挑战性问题以评估模型在真实开放视觉输入下的表现。实验表明现有15个MLLMs在该基准上最高仅达64.0%准确率，揭示了当前模型在视觉理解上的显著不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态基准缺乏足够的视觉多样性，无法有效评估模型在真实复杂视觉环境中的表现，亟需更具代表性和挑战性的评测标准。

Method: 构建跨领域视觉概念分类体系，基于该体系从搜索引擎和现有数据集中采集广泛图像，结合结构化试错方法人工设计难以回答的挑战性问题。

Result: WorldBench在视觉多样性上超越所有现有基准；15个MLLMs平均表现不佳，最强模型仅达64.0%准确率，部分模型接近随机水平。

Conclusion: 视觉多样性是构建高质量多模态评测基准的关键，当前模型在开放世界视觉理解方面仍存在明显短板，需进一步改进。

Abstract: In real-world applications, models are expected to perform reliably across diverse settings. Yet, many existing multimodal benchmarks expand task types without capturing the visual diversity needed to handle open-ended visual inputs. We present WorldBench, a challenging and visually diverse reasoning benchmark to evaluate Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs). We build a taxonomy of thousands of visual concepts across multiple domains (e.g., living things). Guided by this taxonomy, we curate a broad collection of images from search engines and existing datasets to comprehensively represent the visual world. Through structured trial-and-error, we manually design challenging questions that frontier MLLMs fail to answer. On quantitative and human evaluations, WorldBench achieves higher visual diversity than any existing diverse benchmark. Evaluating 15 MLLMs on WorldBench reveals weaknesses in visual understanding: even the strongest model reaches only 64.0% accuracy, while some models perform marginally above chance-level. We hope our work highlights the importance of visual diversity in building multimodal benchmarks.

</details>


### [5] [Synthetic Benchmarks Overstate Forward-Forward Scaling: Real-Data Limits of Layer-Local Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06539)
*Yucheng Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出DTG-FF框架，通过动态温度良度、解耦归一化和多层融合，在九个真实数据集上达到前向-前向（FF）家族的最新水平。研究发现，尽管在32x32小规模数据上FF已接近反向传播（BP），但在真实尺度（如224x224）下其性能显著落后，且随着类别数增加差距扩大；此外，合成任务中FF表现优于BP，但真实图像任务中情况相反，表明合成数据高估了FF的迁移能力；系统层面分析显示，尽管FF无需存储全深度激活，但在8GB硬件上其内存占用与吞吐量均不如标准BP+梯度累积方案，因此当前无法支持以内存优势作为FF替代BP的理由。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究前向-前向（FF）学习在真实数据场景下的可扩展性，评估其是否能在大规模视觉任务中成为反向传播（BP）的有效替代方法。现有研究在32x32小规模数据上取得进展，但缺乏对真实尺度和复杂真实数据分布的系统性验证。

Method: 提出DTG-FF框架，包含动态温度良度（Dynamic Temperature Goodness）、解耦归一化（Decoupled Normalization）和多层融合（Multi-layer Fusion），并在多个真实数据集上进行基准测试，同时设计合成与真实任务对比实验，以及系统资源消耗分析。

Result: 在CIFAR-10和CIFAR-100上，DTG-FF分别达到91.8%和67.5%准确率，是首个在ImageNet-100 224x224上实现的FF基线（49.4%）；然而，与对应架构的BP基线相比仍存在明显差距，且该差距随类别数增加而扩大；合成任务中FF表现更优，但在真实图像任务中则相反；系统实测显示，DTG-FF在内存占用和吞吐量上均劣于标准BP+梯度累积方案。

Conclusion: 尽管FF在小规模任务中表现良好，但在真实数据和大规模任务中仍面临显著性能天花板，且其优势在真实场景下不成立。当前条件下，以内存效率为理由支持FF作为BP替代尚无充分依据，表明层局部训练在现实应用中尚未具备全面可行性。

Abstract: Forward-Forward (FF) learning [Hinton, 2022] replaces backpropagation with strictly layer-local goodness updates. Recent FF-CNN work has narrowed the gap to BP on 32x32 benchmarks, raising the question of whether layer-local training is becoming a viable alternative at realistic scale. To probe this rigorously, we develop DTG-FF -- dynamic temperature goodness, decoupled normalization, and multi-layer fusion -- as an instrument that sets FF-family state of the art across nine real-data benchmarks (91.8% CIFAR-10 and the first FF baseline at ImageNet-100 224x224), and use it to audit how far layer-local training actually scales.
  (1) Real-data scaling. Under identical recipe and backbone, an architecture-matched BP-DeepSup baseline beats DTG-FF by 2.40/5.93 pp on CIFAR-10/CIFAR-100, and the gap widens with class count. At 224x224 the same instrument reaches only 49.4% -- the first FF baseline at this scale, versus typical BP above 75% [Tian et al., 2020] -- exposing a real-data ceiling invisible at 32x32.
  (2) Synthetic vs. real K-conflict. DTG-FF increasingly outperforms BP as class count K grows on synthetic teacher-student tasks, yet on real images the FF-BP gap reverses sign and widens with K. A within-dataset CIFAR-100 coarse vs. fine probe isolates label-hierarchy from image distribution: synthetic K-sweeps confound output dimensionality with fine-grained discrimination difficulty and thereby overstate FF transferability.
  (3) Systems audit. FF can be implemented without storing depth-wide activations, but on commodity 8 GB hardware standard BP+gradient-accumulation reaches 4.18 GB / 157 imgs/s versus DTG-FF's 7.90 GB / 138 imgs/s, so a memory-based justification for FF at this scale is not supported under fair baselines.

</details>


### [6] [Direct 3D-Aware Object Insertion via Decomposed Visual Proxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06601)
*Jingbo Gong,Yikai Wang,Yushi Lan,Yuhao Wan,Ziheng Ouyang,Rui Zhao,Ming-Ming Cheng,Qibin Hou,Chen Change Loy*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: DIRECT 是一种新颖的框架，通过将插入条件分解为外观引导、几何引导和上下文引导三个互补部分，实现可控3D姿态的高质量对象插入。该方法利用独立路径注入各引导信息，避免特征混淆，同时保持参考对象的外观、遵循用户指定的3D姿态并适应目标场景。此外，引入自动化数据构建流程提升训练数据多样性与质量。实验表明，DIRECT在几何可控性和视觉质量方面均优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于扩散的方法将对象插入视为简单的2D修复任务，缺乏对物体3D姿态的显式控制，限制了实际应用。需要一种能够结合交互式姿态调整与高保真2D图像合成的新方法，以实现更灵活、精确的对象插入。

Method: DIRECT 将插入条件分解为三部分：从参考对象中提取的外观引导、由用户调整的3D代理生成的几何引导，以及来自目标背景的上下文引导。通过三条独立路径分别注入这些引导信息，从而避免特征纠缠，并有效保持参考对象的视觉细节、遵循用户设定的3D姿态，同时适配目标场景。还设计了一种自动化数据构造管道以增强训练数据的质量与多样性。

Result: 实验结果显示，DIRECT 在几何可控性与视觉质量方面显著优于现有方法，尤其在复杂姿态和多变背景下的对象插入任务中表现优异。

Conclusion: DIRECT 成功实现了可控3D姿态的高质量对象插入，通过解耦引导信息并引入高质量训练数据，为真实世界应用场景提供了更强的灵活性与实用性。

Abstract: Object insertion aims to seamlessly composite a reference object into a specified region of a background image. Recent diffusion-based methods achieve high visual quality but formulate insertion as a simple 2D inpainting task, providing no explicit control over the object's 3D pose and limiting their practical applicability. We propose DIRECT (Decomposed Injection for Reference Composition and Target-integration), a novel framework that integrates interactive pose manipulation with high-fidelity 2D image synthesis to enable pose-controllable object insertion. Our method decomposes the insertion conditions into three complementary components: appearance guidance capturing visual details from the reference object, geometry guidance derived from the user-adjusted 3D proxy, and context guidance from the target background. By injecting them through separate pathways, DIRECT avoids feature entanglement and simultaneously preserves reference appearance, follows the user-specified pose, and adapts the object to the target scene. We also introduce an automated data construction pipeline to improve the diversity and quality of training data. Experiments show that DIRECT outperforms previous methods in both geometric controllability and visual quality.

</details>


### [7] [From Pixels to Newtons: Predicting In Vivo Joint Contact Forces from Monocular Video](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06631)
*Jessy Lauer*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种无需校准的单目视频分析方法，可实时预测髋关节和膝关节的三维接触力，不依赖标记、力板、肌电图、个体影像或肌肉骨骼模型。通过参数化人体网格提取运动特征，结合自监督视频编码（V-JEPA 2）与变压器架构，实现对多种活动状态下的高精度力估计。在26名患者、25类动作的交叉验证中表现媲美个性化肌肉骨骼模拟（髋关节RMSE 0.32±0.08 BW，膝关节0.23±0.03 BW），并能捕捉细微力变化。零样本迁移至独立仪器化队列仍表现优异，且无需标注动作即可保持准确性，支持原始视频端到端推理。基于预测结果生成的运动先验可生成生物力学合理的低载荷变体，复现已有康复策略。该方法为临床影像回溯分析、初级筛查及家庭康复监测提供了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前关节接触力仅能通过侵入性方式（如植入式传感器）测量，样本量极小，限制了对骨关节炎发展、术后恢复及生物力学干预效果的大规模研究。亟需一种非侵入、低成本、普适性强的方法来估算关节负荷。

Method: 利用未校准的单目视频，通过参数化人体网格重建每帧姿态，提取运动学特征；采用基于自监督视频表征（V-JEPA 2）的变压器模型，融合身体形态、关节类型、肢体侧别、活动文本描述等多源信息，在每一层动态调制姿态流；统一建模髋、膝关节，实现端到端力预测。

Result: 在26名患者、25类活动的留一患者交叉验证中，髋关节预测误差为0.32±0.08 BW RMSE，膝关节为0.23±0.03 BW，达到与个体化肌肉骨骼模拟相当的精度；能识别小于步态训练和骨关节炎进展报告的力变化；零样本迁移至独立数据集表现优于或媲美已有方法；即使无标签视频也能保持高精度，支持原始视频直接推理；生成的运动先验可发现降低峰值负荷的合理运动模式。

Conclusion: 该方法首次实现从未经校准的单目视频中高精度推断髋膝关节接触力，突破传统依赖侵入性测量的瓶颈，为临床回顾分析、基层筛查和居家康复监控开辟全新可能。

Abstract: Joint contact forces govern implant longevity, cartilage health, and rehabilitation outcomes, shaping who develops osteoarthritis, who recovers well from joint replacement, and who benefits from biomechanical interventions. Yet they remain measurable only invasively, in a few dozen patients with instrumented implants. I present a physics-free pipeline to predict instantaneous 3D hip and knee contact forces from an uncalibrated monocular video: no markers, force plates, electromyography, subject-specific imaging, or musculoskeletal model. Parametric body meshes are recovered per frame, encoded as kinematic features, and decoded into forces by a transformer whose pose stream is adaptively modulated at every layer by body shape, joint, side, activity text, and self-supervised video tokens (V-JEPA 2), unifying hip and knee in a single model. Under leave-one-subject-out cross-validation across 26 patients and 25 activity categories from the in vivo OrthoLoad database, the pipeline matches the accuracy of subject-specific musculoskeletal simulations ($0.32 \pm 0.08$ BW RMSE for hip; $0.23 \pm 0.03$ BW for knee) and resolves peak force changes smaller than those reported for gait retraining and osteoarthritis progression. Applied zero-shot to an independent instrumented cohort, it rivals or outperforms prior published methods. Even without curated activity labels, video features alone preserve accuracy and enable end-to-end inference on raw footage. Driven by the predictor, a generative motion prior produces biomechanically plausible variants with reduced peak loading, rediscovering strategies from the predictive simulation literature. This pipeline establishes uncalibrated monocular video as a viable modality for estimating joint loading, opening a path toward retrospective analysis of archived clinical recordings, primary-care screening, and at-home rehabilitation tracking.

</details>

### [9] [Architecture-Adaptive Uncertainty Fusion for Deepfake Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06666)
*Ritesh Sharma,Mohammad Ghasemigol,Yuichi Motai*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Correlation-Optimized Fusion（COF）框架，通过最大化融合不确定性得分与预测误差之间的皮尔逊相关性，自适应地融合五种互补的不确定性来源（认知、随机、校准、置信区间、分布），在无需修改模型的情况下实现高效不确定性量化。相比传统深度集成需20-45小时训练，COF仅需42秒权重优化。在FaceForensics++上，非线性方法在同分布下相关性略优（均值r=0.438），但在分布外场景下COF显著胜出；在CelebDF上，COF在9/11架构中超越随机森林，最大相关性提升7.3倍。跨数据集评估显示所有方法均出现灾难性泛化失效，平均退化达90.7%，七种架构出现不确定性反转。结果表明，COF适用于受控分布部署，而领域自适应不确定性量化是法证应用的核心挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有不确定性量化方法依赖单一来源，未考虑不同模型架构下最优不确定性组合差异，导致在真实部署中缺乏可靠预测不确定性，尤其在分布外或跨数据集场景下表现严重退化。

Method: 提出一种基于约束优化的概率单纯形上的融合策略——Correlation-Optimized Fusion（COF），通过最大化五类不确定性源（epistemic, aleatoric, calibration, conformal, distributional）的融合得分与实际预测误差间的皮尔逊相关性，实现架构自适应的不确定性融合。该方法不需模型修改，计算高效。

Result: 在十一种架构上评估表明：在同分布条件下，非线性方法相关性略高（平均r=0.438），但分布外性能差；在CelebDF上，COF在9/11架构中优于随机森林，最大相关性提升7.3倍；跨数据集评估中，所有方法均出现近90%的相关性下降，7个架构发生不确定性反转，凸显当前方法泛化能力不足。

Conclusion: COF是一种高效、可解释的不确定性量化框架，适用于受控分布下的法证部署；然而，如何实现领域自适应的不确定性量化，仍是当前法证应用面临的核心挑战。

Abstract: Deepfake detection systems achieve near-perfect accuracy on benchmarks, yet forensic deployment demands reliable prediction uncertainty. Existing uncertainty quantification (UQ) methods rely on single sources and ignore that optimal uncertainty composition varies across architectures. We propose Correlation-Optimized Fusion (COF), an architecture-adaptive framework that fuses five complementary uncertainty sources -- epistemic, aleatoric, calibration, conformal, and distributional -- by maximizing Pearson correlation between fused uncertainty scores and prediction errors via constrained optimization on the probability simplex. COF requires no model modifications and only 42 s of weight optimization, compared to 20--45 h for a 5-model Deep Ensemble. Evaluation across eleven architectures on FaceForensics++ reveals a fundamental trade-off: under matched train/evaluation protocol, non-linear methods achieve approximately 5--6% higher in-domain correlation than COF (mean r = 0.438), but this reverses under distribution shift. On CelebDF, COF outperforms Random Forest in 9/11 architectures with up to 7.3x higher correlation (MaxViT-B: r = 0.249 vs. 0.034); RF degrades 85% cross-domain to r = 0.071, whereas COF retains substantially more signal (74% drop to r = 0.116). Cross-dataset evaluation on CelebDF and DFDC reveals catastrophic generalization failure across all methods: in-domain correlations of 0.41--0.47 collapse to near-zero externally (mean degradation 90.7%), with seven of eleven architectures exhibiting uncertainty inversion. These results establish COF as a practical, interpretable framework for controlled-distribution deployment and identify domain-adaptive UQ as the central open challenge for forensic deployment.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于经典谱分析，利用目标信号的离散正弦变换（DST）与雅可比-安格展开，推导出两层正弦MLP的闭式权重，使网络初始频谱响应与目标信号解析匹配，无需随机种子或额外超参数调优。

Abstract: Existing implicit neural representation (INR) approaches suffer from stochastic initialization that does not guarantee consistent or high-quality performance across runs, with variations reaching more than 2.5 dB (78%) in image regression. This variation is problematic for scientific computing and simulation, where result reproducibility is crucial. To address this problem, we present Jacobi-Anger Sinusoidal Representation Network (JA-SIREN), a deterministic initialization scheme for sinusoidal networks grounded in classical spectral analysis. By computing the Discrete Sine Transform (DST) of the target signal and leveraging the Jacobi-Anger expansion, we derive closed-form weights for a two-layer sinusoidal MLP that analytically match the network's initial spectral response to the target signal, requiring no random seed or additional hyperparameter tuning. On the Kodak dataset, JA-SIREN achieves a mean PSNR of 67.18 dB, a 21.30 dB improvement over the best baseline. This is achieved with zero run-to-run variance, confirming that spectrally-informed initialization is a more effective and reproducible alternative to stochastic initialization for sinusoidal INRs.

### [11] [Adaptive Band Selection for Hyperspectral Classification with Spatially Disjoint Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06684)
*Ikram El-Hajri,Ouassim Karrakchou,Alejandro Mousist*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SGBR-HC是一种两阶段的超光谱波段选择方法，通过监督式光谱排名初始化可训练的稀疏门控，避免对固定波段数量的依赖。第一阶段基于类别可区分性和光谱多样性对候选波段进行评分，为第二阶段提供门控初始值；第二阶段联合训练稀疏门控与空间分类器。在Pavia University和Houston 2013数据集上，该方法在空间不重叠评估下表现优异，使用约20个波段即达到最高平均总体精度和Cohen's kappa值。移除第一阶段导致性能显著下降，证明了先验排名的重要性；随机像素划分则引入严重空间泄露偏差，影响评估可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于可微分选择器的超光谱波段选择方法对初始化敏感，且固定波段数量限制灵活性。需要一种更鲁棒、自适应波段数的方法，并避免评估中的空间泄露问题。

Method: 提出SGBR-HC方法：第一阶段通过监督式光谱排名生成候选波段的得分，作为稀疏门控的初始值；第二阶段联合训练稀疏门控与空间分类器，使最终选择的波段数量由训练过程决定。采用硬-混凝土（Hard-Concrete）初始化以实现稀疏性约束。

Result: 在Pavia University和Houston 2013数据集上，SGBR-HC在空间不重叠评估下实现了最高的平均总体精度和Cohen's kappa值，仅需约20个波段即可达到最优性能。移除第一阶段导致性能下降8.84个百分点（Pavia）和22.15个百分点（Houston），表明先验排名的关键作用；随机划分导致精度虚高30.56个百分点，凸显空间泄露的危害。

Conclusion: SGBR-HC通过结合监督式光谱排名与可训练稀疏门控，有效提升了波段选择的鲁棒性与灵活性，同时避免了固定波段数和空间泄露问题，是高效且可靠的超光谱波段选择方案。

Abstract: Hyperspectral band selection methods based on differentiable selectors can be sensitive to initialization and to extracting a final discrete subset, while prescribed band counts limit flexibility. We propose SGBR-HC (Spectral-Group Band Ranking with Hard-Concrete initialization), a two-stage method that uses a supervised spectral ranking to initialize trainable sparse gates rather than treating ranking as a fixed selection rule, letting the number of selected bands be determined by training. Stage-1 scores candidate bands from training pixels by class discriminability and spectral diversity; this ranking seeds the gate logits for Stage-2, which trains the sparse gates jointly with a spatial classifier. Under spatially disjoint evaluation on Pavia University and Houston 2013, verified by retraining a fresh classifier on the selected bands, SGBR-HC achieves the highest mean overall accuracy and Cohen's kappa with approximately twenty bands. Bypassing Stage-1 degrades OA by 8.84 pp on Pavia University and 22.15 pp on Houston 2013, confirming the ranking prior's role. Random pixel splits inflate OA on Pavia University by 30.56 pp, underscoring spatial leakage as a critical evaluation confound.

### [12] [RigPAPR: Rig-Based Animation of Static Neural Point Clouds from a Fixed-Viewpoint Video](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06685)
*Shichong Peng,Yanshu Zhang,Ke Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: RigPAPR 通过自动为静态的 PAPR 点云生成骨骼并直接使用线性混合皮肤（LBS）驱动单视角视频，无需网格代理或姿态依赖修正，有效避免了关节边界处的间隙与尖刺伪影，在合成与真实数据上均实现了更优的渲染质量，尤其在新视角下表现显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在动画化静态神经点重建时，采用直接线性混合皮肤（LBS）或网格代理，导致关节边界出现间隙和尖刺等伪影，问题根源在于每个点球携带独立的静止形状，无法随运动自然调整；而传统点云渲染在变形时缺乏表面自适应能力。

Method: 提出 RigPAPR：基于无固定形状的邻近注意力点渲染（PAPR），在渲染时动态重组点位置以适应形变；结合自动骨骼生成与直接 LBS 驱动，无需网格代理、姿态修正或类别模板，实现高保真且无伪影的动画重建。

Result: 在合成数据上，RigPAPR 在监督视角下达到最强基线性能，在新视角下比基于网格和高斯点云的方法提升超过 3dB PSNR；真实与合成主体的关节边界渲染更加清晰，无明显伪影。

Abstract: Static neural point reconstructions capture a subject at high fidelity from posed images. Given such a reconstruction, we aim to animate it to follow a monocular fixed-viewpoint driving video of the subject, whether captured or produced by image-to-video (I2V) generation, and to recover a rigged, re-posable 3D asset. Existing methods deform Gaussian splats through direct linear blend skinning (LBS) or mesh proxies, both of which are prone to joint-boundary artifacts under articulation, even with per-primitive corrections. We trace the artifact to the representation: each splat carries an individual shape calibrated in the canonical pose to tile with its neighbours. Under rigid LBS, each splat moves with its bone but cannot bend, so the canonical tiling breaks at joint boundaries into gaps and spikes. Proximity attention point rendering (PAPR) instead carries no per-primitive shape; each pixel is recomposed at render time from the deformed primitives' positions, so the surface re-forms naturally with the articulation. We present RigPAPR, which auto-rigs a static PAPR cloud and drives it under direct LBS from a single fixed-viewpoint video, without mesh proxy, pose-dependent correction, or category template. On synthetic subjects, RigPAPR matches the strongest baseline at the supervised view and exceeds mesh-based and Gaussian-splatting baselines at novel views by 3+dB PSNR, with cleaner joint-boundary renderings of both synthetic and real subjects.

### [13] [RPC-GS: Gaussian Splatting with native RPC Rendering for Satellite Imagery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06690)
*Valentin Wagner,Sebastian Bullinger,Christoph Bodensteiner,Michael Arens*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: RPC-GS是首个原生支持理性多项式相机（RPC）模型的高斯点云渲染框架，专为卫星影像设计。它避免了以往方法中用透视或仿射模型近似RPC带来的几何误差，通过直接在点云投射过程中使用RPC模型，并结合数值稳定的雅可比协方差投影与基于度量射线的深度建模，在多个主流卫星数据集上显著降低重建误差，优于透视和仿射模型，分别在DFC2019上提升29.6%和63.8%，在IARPA2016上提升9.9%和37.9%。代码已开源，推动卫星图像领域高斯点云研究发展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出RPC-GS框架，将RPC模型嵌入一系列精心选择的地理坐标变换链中，实现从场景坐标到图像坐标的映射；针对高斯协方差矩阵的投影，推导出一种数值稳定的基于雅可比的协方差传播方法；由于RPC模型无显式相机深度，引入基于度量射线的深度建模机制，从而实现高精度、无近似的卫星图像渲染。

Result: 在DFC2019和IARPA2016两个主流卫星基准数据集上，RPC-GS在统一框架下表现最优，其平均高度误差相比透视模型分别降低29.6%和9.9%，相比仿射模型分别降低63.8%和37.9%，验证了其优越的重建精度和对真实几何结构的忠实还原能力。

Conclusion: RPC-GS首次实现了卫星影像中高斯点云对理性多项式相机模型的原生支持，通过精确的坐标变换与协方差传播策略，显著提升了三维重建精度，为未来卫星图像的高效、高保真可视化与分析提供了坚实基础，代码已公开，促进该领域的持续研究。

Abstract: We present RPC-GS, the first Gaussian Splatting framework for satellite imagery that operates natively with Rational Polynomial Camera (RPC) models. The RPC model is the de facto standard for representing the complex imaging geometry of modern pushbroom satellite sensors. To simplify rendering, prior satellite Gaussian Splatting methods replace the RPC model with perspective or affine camera approximations, leading to geometric errors during reconstruction. RPC-GS avoids these approximations by projecting Gaussian means and covariances directly through the RPC model during the splatting process. We embed the RPC model in a chain of carefully selected geo-coordinate transformations representing a mapping from splatting-suitable scene coordinates to image coordinates. To map the Gaussian covariance matrices, we derive a numerically robust Jacobian-based covariance projection for the (partially nonlinear) coordinate transformations. Since RPCs lack an explicit notion of camera depth, we integrate a metric ray-based depth formulation. We benchmark RPC, perspective, and affine camera models in a unified framework, with our native RPC renderer consistently achieving the lowest reconstruction error on leading satellite benchmark datasets, improving mean altitude error over perspective and affine approximations by 29.6% and 63.8% on DFC2019, and by 9.9% and 37.9% on IARPA2016. We release our code to support future research of Gaussian Splatting in the satellite imaging domain.

Motivation: 当前生物医学视觉语言模型的评估基准有限，无法充分衡量模型在细微特征识别和跨模态泛化能力上的表现，亟需更全面的评估体系。

It is the largest biomedical vision and language benchmark to date, covering 35 submodalities with rich structured metadata. ### [16] [USU-Corn-WeedDB: A UAV RGB Image Dataset for Multi-Species Weed Detection in Forage Corn](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06709)
*Utsav Bhandari,Saroj Burlakoti,Rhonda Miller,Sierra Young,Eric Westra,Aaron Etienne*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究提出USU-Corn-WeedDB，一个公开的无人机RGB图像数据集，用于支持玉米田中多种杂草的检测。数据集来自犹他州卡斯山谷的一个商业玉米田，使用Autel EVO II Dual 640T V2无人机在2025年6月27日采集，飞行高度约10米，地面采样距离约为0.48厘米/像素。共获取366张全分辨率图像，分割为8,800个640×640像素的图像块，其中800张图像经人工标注，涵盖三种杂草（藜、红根苋、绿狗尾草），共10,539个边界框实例；其余8,000个图像块作为无标签数据用于半监督学习。数据集保留了真实田间条件下杂草分布的自然类别不平衡（红根苋占53.86%）。通过在28个不同架构的检测模型上进行测试，包括YOLOv8、YOLOv9、YOLOv10、YOLO11、YOLO26和RT-DETR，未进行超参数调优的情况下，mAP@0.5范围为0.773至0.840，轻量级模型表现出与边缘部署无人机系统兼容的优异性能。该数据集已公开发布于https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.20044178。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于无人机影像和深度学习的精准杂草管理（SSWM）受限于缺乏代表性田野训练数据集，尤其在多类杂草检测方面。为解决这一问题，构建一个真实农田场景下具有代表性的公开数据集，以支持监督与半监督学习框架下的杂草检测研究。

Method: 采用无人机（Autel EVO II Dual 640T V2）在商业玉米田上采集高分辨率RGB影像，飞行高度约10米，生成地面采样距离约0.48厘米/像素的图像。将366张全图切分为8,800个640×640像素的图像块，其中800张进行人工标注，涵盖三种主要杂草物种；其余8,000个图像块作为无标签数据池。数据集设计中保留了实际田间杂草分布的自然类别不平衡特征。使用28种不同架构的目标检测模型（如YOLO系列和RT-DETR）在相同条件下训练并评估，验证数据集的有效性。

Result: 在未进行超参数调优的情况下，所训练的28个目标检测模型在测试集上的mAP@0.5值介于0.773到0.840之间，表明数据集具备良好的泛化能力。轻量级模型也展现出适用于边缘部署无人机系统的高性能，证明该数据集在实际应用中的可行性。

Conclusion: USU-Corn-WeedDB是一个真实、高质量、公开可用的无人机图像数据集，能够有效支持针对玉米田杂草的多类检测任务，尤其适用于监督与半监督学习方法。其在真实田间条件下的结构设计提升了模型在实际农业场景中的适用性，为未来精准农业中的智能杂草管理提供了重要基础资源。

Abstract: Weed pressure in forage corn production causes yield losses of up to 31.5%, yet site-specific weed management (SSWM) systems built on UAV imagery and deep learning remain constrained by the scarcity of field-representative training datasets. We present USU-Corn-WeedDB, a publicly available UAV RGB image dataset collected from a commercial forage corn field in Cache Valley, Utah, designed to support multi-class weed detection under both supervised and semi-supervised learning frameworks. RGB imagery was acquired on 27 June 2025 using an Autel EVO II Dual 640T V2 drone at ~10m above ground level, yielding a ground sampling distance of approximately 0.48 cm/pixel. A total of 366 full-resolution images were tiled into 8,800 patches at 640 x 640-pixel resolution. Of these, 800 images were manually annotated for three weed species; common lambsquarters (Chenopodium album), redroot pigweed (Amaranthus retroflexus), and green foxtail (Setaria viridis) comprising 10,539 bounding-box instances, with the remaining 8,000 tiles retained as an unlabeled pool for semi-supervised experiments. This dataset reflects a natural class imbalance where redroot pigweed constitutes 53.86% of annotated instances, which was preserved intentionally to mirror real field conditions. To validate dataset utility, we trained 28 object detection models spanning five architecture families including YOLOv8, YOLOv9, YOLOv10, YOLO11, YOLO26, and RT-DETR under identical conditions without hyperparameter tuning. Test set mAP@0.5 ranged from 0.773 to 0.840, with lightweight models achieving competitive performance relevant to edge-deployed UAV systems. USU-Corn-WeedDB is publicly available at https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.20044178.

### [17] [Anchored, Not Graded: Vision-Language Models Fail at Slant-from-Texture Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06714)
*Qian Zhang,Michal Golovanevsky,Fulvio Domini,James Tompkin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了视觉语言模型（VLMs）在感知表面倾角任务中的表现，发现其在零样本和上下文提示下表现出明显的锚定偏差，仅对特定倾角（如0°、±25°、±45°）做出预测，且对视场、光学倾角和曲率不敏感。监督微调部分缓解了这一问题，但锚定现象仍存在。研究认为，这种现象反映了模型在从表示到语言输出接口上的失败，而非缺乏几何编码能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究视觉语言模型（VLMs）是否具备类似人类对表面倾角的感知能力，尤其是其对低级几何线索的敏感性。

Method: 通过多种VLM家族和不同规模的模型，在零样本和上下文提示条件下评估其对表面倾角的预测表现，并对比监督微调后的效果。

Result: 所有VLMs均表现出显著的倾角锚定现象，仅对少数固定角度进行预测，且对输入刺激变化不敏感；监督微调虽有改善，但锚定现象依然存在。

Conclusion: VLMs在表达几何信息时存在缺陷，表现为无法以连续、渐进的方式输出倾角，这表明其在表示与语言输出之间的映射存在问题，而非缺乏几何感知能力。

Abstract: Human perception of surface slant from texture exhibits systematic, graded biases that emerge reliably in psychophysical experiments. Prior work showed that unsupervised CNNs reproduce several human-like biases, while supervised CNNs do not. Do Vision-Language Models (VLMs) exhibit similar competences? Across multiple VLM families and model scales, zero-shot and in-context prompting both produce distinctive failures: slant is predicted at only a small set of anchors (e.g., 0\degree, $\pm$25\degree, $\pm$45\degree) with little dependence on stimulus field of view, optical slant, or surface curvature. Supervised fine-tuning partially remediates the failure, but residual anchoring persists. While success in high-level vision-language benchmarks might not require sensitivity to low-level geometric cues, we interpret anchoring as a failure at the representation-to-output language interface: Not necessarily an absence of geometric encoding, but a failure to express it in a graded form.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有医学视觉语言模型难以同时具备精准的视觉理解与分割能力，限制了其在临床推理中的应用。需要一种能够将视觉发现与语义解释有效连接的统一框架。

Method: 提出 Region Perceiver 模块生成以区域为中心的特征表示，并设计医学区域码本嵌入大语言模型词汇表中，使模型能生成离散的解剖或病理区域代码；通过代码反向重建分割掩膜，实现空间接地；结合渐进式训练策略，逐步对齐各模块。

Result: 在多种成像模态下，仅使用72,000个多模态指令对训练，MedSIGHT 在医学理解与分割任务上均达到当前最优性能。

Abstract: Medical large vision-language models (Med-LVLMs) have recently achieved remarkable progress in vision-language comprehension and medical image segmentation. However, existing models still struggle to unify these two capabilities, which is essential for achieving clinically reasoning that connects visual findings with semantic interpretation. We present MedSIGHT, a unified framework that equips Med-LVLMs with structured, pixel-level understanding for grounded visual comprehension. MedSIGHT introduces a novel Region Perceiver module that produces region-centric tokens, encoding spatial information directly into representation space of the language model. We further propose a medical region codebook into the LLM vocabulary, allowing the model to generate discrete region codes as symbolic representations of anatomical and pathological regions. These codes are decoded through the Region Perceiver to reconstruct segmentation mask, achieving end-to-end spatial grounding. Lastly, MedSIGHT combines Region Perceiver, Codebook and LLM using our proposed progressive training strategy to gradually aligns these modules stably. Trained on only 72K multimodal instruction pairs, MedSIGHT achieves state-of-the-art performance across diverse imaging modalities on both medical comprehension and segmentation tasks.

### [19] [Breaking the Lock-in: Diversifying Text-to-Image Generation via Representation Modulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06813)
*Dahee Kwon,Haeun Lee,Jaesik Choi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文提出DAVE方法，通过在生成早期阶段有选择性地衰减Transformer特征中的零频空间平均（DC）成分，实现无需训练的多样性增强。该方法避免了昂贵的采样或辅助优化，保持了高质量图像生成能力的同时显著提升了同一提示下的样本多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本到图像生成模型在固定提示下常产生过于相似的样本，尽管已有多样性增强方法，但通常需要高成本的采样或额外优化，带来显著开销。因此，亟需一种高效且无需训练的解决方案来提升多样性。

Method: 通过分析Transformer中间特征，发现零频空间平均（DC）成分在生成早期快速收敛，导致轨迹过早锁定，限制了多样性。基于此，提出DAVE方法，在早期阶段对DC成分进行选择性衰减，从而打破早期同质化，提升生成多样性。

Result: DAVE在不改变原有采样流程的前提下，实现了显著的多样性提升，同时保持了与现有方法相当甚至更优的图像质量，且几乎无额外计算开销。

Conclusion: DAVE是一种高效的、无需训练的多样性增强方法，通过干预特征表示层面的早期动态，有效缓解了文本到图像生成中因轨迹锁死导致的同质化问题，为高质量、多样化生成提供了新思路。

Abstract: Recent text-to-image models built on large-scale Transformer backbones and flow-based objectives deliver strong text-image alignment and high visual quality, yet often produce overly similar samples under a fixed prompt. Existing diversity-enhancement methods alleviate this issue, but typically require expensive sampling or auxiliary optimization, incurring non-trivial overhead. To investigate the root cause of this homogeneity, we examine intermediate Transformer features and observe that the zero-frequency spatial average (DC) component rapidly converges across seeds early in generation, causing early trajectory lock-in that limits downstream variation. Building on this observation, we propose DC Attenuation for diVersity Enhancement (DAVE), a training-free representation-level intervention that selectively attenuates this component in the early regime. DAVE preserves the sampling pipeline with negligible overhead, improving prompt-consistent diversity while maintaining competitive image quality.

### [20] [VideoSEG-O3: A Multi-turn Reinforcement Learning Framework for Reasoning Video Object Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06819)
*Ming Dai,Sen Yang,Boqiang Duan,Boyuan Tong,Jiedong Zhuang,Wankou Yang,Jingdong Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: VideoSEG-O3 是首个用于推理视频对象分割（RVOS）的多轮强化学习框架，模拟人类从粗到细的认知过程。它通过多轮时空思维链捕捉细粒度细节，利用视觉证据迭代定位关键片段和帧，并引入感知分割质量的对数校准机制，以提升模型在强化学习阶段的反馈精度。同时，设计了解耦的思维轨迹，将推理过程分解为时间、空间和语言维度，并构建了专门的冷启动数据集 VTS-CoT，支持复杂参考的精准定位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法仅依赖固定初始输入进行推理，缺乏主动获取额外视觉证据的能力，难以应对长视频或复杂引用中的精细定位需求。为此，需要一种能动态获取信息并逐步优化推理过程的新框架。

Method: 提出 VideoSEG-O3 框架，采用多轮强化学习机制，结合多轮时空思维链（Temporal-Spatial Chain-of-Thought），迭代识别关键时间区间与关键帧；引入 SEG-aware logit calibration，将像素级分割反馈融入词元级对数概率；设计 decoupled thinking trace 实现时间、空间、语言维度的分层推理，并构建 VTS-CoT 数据集以支持冷启动训练。

Result: 在多个基准数据集上显著优于现有方法，特别是在处理复杂引用和长视频时表现突出，证明了多轮交互与细粒度推理的有效性。

Conclusion: VideoSEG-O3 通过模拟人类认知的渐进式推理方式，实现了对复杂视频语义引用的精准像素级定位，为未来智能视频理解提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Reasoning Video Object Segmentation (RVOS) demands a sophisticated integration of temporal dynamics, spatial details, and linguistic reasoning to achieve precise pixel-level localization. Existing methods are limited to reasoning over fixed initial inputs and lack the capacity to actively acquire further visual evidence, which is often essential for resolving complex references in long or intricate videos. To address this, we propose \textbf{VideoSEG-O3}, the first multi-turn reinforcement learning framework for RVOS that emulates the human \textit{``coarse-to-fine''} cognitive process. It employs a \textit{multi-turn temporal-spatial chain-of-thought} to capture fine-grained details by iteratively pinpointing critical intervals and keyframes. Additionally, to enable the policy to perceive segmentation quality beyond mere text probability of \texttt{[SEG]} during the RL stage, we introduce \textit{SEG-aware logit calibration}, which integrates pixel-wise segmentation feedback directly into the token-level logits. Furthermore, we design a \textit{decoupled thinking trace} to hierarchically decompose the reasoning process into temporal, spatial, and linguistic dimensions, and construct \textbf{VTS-CoT}, a specialized cold-start dataset featuring comprehensive reasoning trajectories. The code and models will be released at https://github.com/Dmmm1997/VideoSEG-O3.

### [21] [AdaGRPO: A Capability-Aware Adaptive Enhancement for Flow-based GRPO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06828)
*Jiazi Bu,Pengyang Ling,Yujie Zhou,Yibin Wang,Yuhang Zang,Tianyi Wei,Xiaohang Zhan,Jiaqi Wang,Tong Wu,Xingang Pan,Dahua Lin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AdaGRPO提出一种能力感知的强化学习算法，解决现有流模型中GRPO在提示选择和优势估计上的盲点问题。通过在线课程过滤策略动态匹配模型当前学习边界，并结合跨层级优势融合实现更全面的策略评估，可无缝集成至现有框架并显著提升性能与训练稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有flow-based GRPO方法在提示选择上随机采样，忽略数据选择对RL效果的关键影响；且仅依赖组内统计评估样本质量，缺乏全局视角，导致优势估计不准确。

Method: 提出AdaGRPO，包含两个核心组件：(i) 在线课程过滤策略，动态跟踪模型能力并自适应选择匹配当前学习边界的提示；(ii) 跨层级优势融合，整合细粒度组内优势与宏观全局优势，实现无偏策略评估。

Result: 实验表明，AdaGRPO能持续提升性能，显著稳定GRPO训练过程，作为轻量级模块可无缝集成于Flow-GRPO、DanceGRPO、Flow-CPS等框架。

Conclusion: AdaGRPO通过能力感知的提示选择与全局优势融合机制，有效弥补了现有GRPO方法在学习循环中的关键缺陷，为流模型的偏好对齐提供了更高效、稳定的解决方案。

Abstract: Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) has demonstrated remarkable success in aligning text-to-image (T2I) flow models with human preferences. However, we have identified that the learning loop of current flow-based GRPO is fundamentally decoupled from the learner's current capability, suffering from critical blind spots at both prompt selection and advantage estimation: (i) Existing methods sample prompts randomly, overlooking the substantial impact of data selection on reinforcement learning (RL) efficacy--a factor proven crucial in GRPO for large language models; (ii) They evaluate sample quality solely relying on intra-group statistics, lacking a global perspective to accurately measure true policy improvement. To address these issues, we propose Adaptive GRPO (AdaGRPO), a novel capability-aware RL algorithm tailored for flow models. Specifically, AdaGRPO consists of two principal components: (i) Online Curriculum Filtering Strategy: Dynamically tracks the model's proficiency and adaptively selects prompts that best match its current learning boundary; (ii) Cross-Level Advantage Fusion: Synergistically integrates fine-grained intra-group advantages with macro-level global advantages, providing a comprehensive and unbiased policy evaluation. As a lightweight, plug-and-play module, AdaGRPO can be seamlessly integrated with existing frameworks such as Flow-GRPO, DanceGRPO, and Flow-CPS. Extensive experiments demonstrate that AdaGRPO consistently drives performance gains while significantly stabilizes GRPO training for flow models.

### [22] [CFRNet: Cycle-Consistent Fixed-Point Training for Real-Time Blind Face Restoration on Consumer Embedded NPUs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06850)
*Fuchen Li,Xinyang Wang,Yahui Zhang,Yuhan Chen,Jiahong Guo,Zhuohan Qin,Wenbo Ma*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CFRNet 是一种专为消费级设备设计的轻量级面部修复网络，采用循环一致的固定点训练（CCFP）方法，在保持低延迟和低内存占用的同时实现高图像质量。它在 256×256 分辨率下仅需 2.0M 参数，通过三重损失函数训练，使模型在多次迭代后趋于稳定（固定点），无需额外计算开销。实验表明其在 LPIPS、PSNR 和 SSIM 指标上均优于 GFPGAN、CodeFormer 等现有方法，并可在 HiSilicon Hi3402 NPU 上以约 23ms/周期运行，支持实时部署。此外，该方法可扩展至更简单的 CNN 结构，适用于车载驾驶员监控等实际场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前主流的强性能面部修复方法（如 GFPGAN、CodeFormer）依赖于大型生成先验和复杂操作（如注意力机制、代码本查找、风格调制），难以在消费级小规模神经处理单元（NPU）上高效编译与量化。而小型卷积网络虽速度快，但常导致过度平滑及眼鼻口区域伪影。因此，亟需一种兼顾高质量、低延迟与易部署的轻量级面部修复方案，以适配移动端和嵌入式设备。

Method: 提出 CFRNet，基于循环一致的固定点训练（CCFP）策略。通过引入三种训练损失：渐进多循环监督、幂等性损失（idempotence loss）和再退化循环损失，使网络在多次应用后输出不再变化，即成为固定点算子。该训练方式不增加推理成本，且支持通过调整循环次数 $k$ 实现质量可调。同时，所有基线模型均在相同 256×256 分辨率下重新训练，确保公平对比。

Result: 在 300 张图像测试集上，CFRNet 在三轮循环下达到最低 LPIPS 值（0.250，相比单轮降低 31%），并取得最优的 PSNR 与 SSIM 表现；在 HiSilicon Hi3402 NPU 上以 INT8 精度运行时，每轮耗时约 23ms，显著优于无法编译到该芯片的基线模型。循环次数 $k=2$ 时 PSNR 最佳，而 LPIPS 可持续提升至 $k=3$，表明其具备灵活的质量调节能力。进一步验证了该方法在简化版 CNN 上的有效性，并成功实现在车载驾驶监控系统的实时运行。

Conclusion: CFRNet 通过循环一致的固定点训练策略，实现了在消费级设备上高性能、低延迟、易部署的面部修复能力。其核心思想无需额外推理开销即可达成高质量恢复，且可通过调节循环次数动态控制质量，具有良好的实用价值和推广潜力。

Abstract: Blind face restoration on consumer devices has to balance image quality against speed and memory. Strong methods such as GFPGAN and CodeFormer give good perceptual quality, but they rely on large pretrained generative priors and on operators such as attention, codebook lookup, and style modulation that are hard to compile and quantize on the small neural processing units (NPUs) used in consumer hardware. Small convolutional restorers run fast enough, but they tend to over-smooth and to leave artifacts around the eyes, nose, and mouth. We present CFRNet, a 2.0,M-parameter ResNet-style restorer for on-device use at $256\times256$, the common face-crop size on consumer NPUs. The main idea is Cycle-Consistent Fixed-Point Training (CCFP). Instead of training the network for one pass and then running it several times by hand, we train it to act as a fixed-point operator, so that applying it again to a restored face does not change the face. CCFP uses three training losses, namely progressive multi-cycle supervision, an idempotence loss, and a re-degradation cycle loss, and it adds no cost at inference. To compare fairly under our deployment limits, we retrain all baselines from scratch at the same $256\times256$ resolution. On a 300-image test set, CFRNet reaches the best perceptual score (LPIPS 0.250 at three cycles, which is 31% lower than one cycle) and also the best PSNR and SSIM at two cycles. It runs in about 23,ms per cycle in INT8 on a HiSilicon Hi3402 NPU, while the same baselines cannot be compiled to that chip. The cycle count $k$ acts as a simple quality knob that needs no retraining: PSNR is best at $k\!=\!2$ and LPIPS keeps improving up to $k\!=\!3$. We further show that the same idea works with a plain CNN that is even easier to deploy, and we run the model in real time on an in-car driver-monitoring board.

</details>


### [23] [MotionEnhancer: Leveraging Video Diffusion for Motion-Enhanced Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06853)
*Yifan Xu,Chao Zhang,Ruifei Ma,Fei Gao,Zhifei Yang,Jiaxing Qi,Zhipeng Chen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前视觉语言模型（VLMs）在事件或故事级理解方面表现良好，但在捕捉细粒度运动细节方面能力有限，主要因其关注高层静态语义结构和宏观事件逻辑。而视频扩散模型（VDMs）擅长建模动态运动模式，具备生成时序数据的能力。因此，需要一种方法将VDM中的运动先验有效引入到VLM中，以提升其运动理解能力。

Method: MotionEnhancer采用两个参数无关的模块：运动敏感头选择（MHS）用于识别与运动相关的注意力头，运动显著文本标记识别（MTTI）用于定位与运动相关的文本标记；二者结合通过注意力对齐方式，将来自VDM的运动先验作为辅助监督注入VLM，实现运动理解能力的增强。整个过程无需额外训练参数、不改变原有架构、无需工具调用。

Result: 在两个运动级视频理解基准测试中，MotionEnhancer均显著优于现有最先进方法，尤其是在运动相关评价指标上表现出明显提升，验证了其在增强细粒度运动理解方面的有效性。

Conclusion: MotionEnhancer是一种高效且可扩展的方案，能够无需额外训练或架构修改，利用视频扩散模型中的运动先验显著提升视觉语言模型在运动理解任务上的表现，为多模态视频理解提供了新的思路。

Abstract: The new era has witnessed a remarkable capability to extend Vision-Language Models (VLMs) for tackling tasks of video understanding. While current VLMs excel at event- or story-level understanding, their ability to capture fine-grained motion details remains limited, primarily due to their focus on high-level static semantic structures and macro-event logic. In contrast, Video Diffusion Models (VDMs) are adept at modeling dynamic motion patterns, benefiting from large-scale video data and the intrinsic requirement of temporal generation. In this paper, we introduce MotionEnhancer, a novel approach that leverages motion priors distilled from a powerful video diffusion model as auxiliary supervision to enhance the motion understanding capability of a VLM via attention alignment. MotionEnhancer comprises two simple parameter-free modules, Motion-sensitive Head Selection (MHS) and Motion-salient Text Token Identification (MTTI), to directly extract and optimize motion-related attentions from the VDM in a computation-only manner. MotionEnhancer provides a scalable solution for motion understanding without additional training parameters, modifications to existing architectures, or tool calling. Extensive experiments demonstrate that MotionEnhancer can achieve consistent improvements over state-of-the-art VLMs on two motion-level video understanding benchmarks, especially on motion-related metrics.

### [24] [FS-DVS: A Frequency-Selective Dynamic Visual Sensing Paradigm for Enhancing Information Completeness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06856)
*Feiyu Ji,Xiaokang Yang,Xiaoyun Yuan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出FS-DVS，一种新型动态视觉传感器，通过在事件触发前引入可学习的空间滤波器，模拟视网膜神经节细胞的聚合机制，实现对中频空间频率的选择性增强，显著提升目标检测与动作识别性能，并自发形成类人对比敏感度函数（CSF）特征，具有高噪声鲁棒性和生物合理性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统DVS采用像素级独立触发机制，忽略生物视网膜神经节细胞的空间整合能力，导致缺乏对比敏感度函数（CSF）特性，尤其对中频空间频率不敏感，造成亚阈值信号丢失和信息不完整。

Method: 设计FS-DVS，引入可学习的空间滤波器置于事件触发前，结合可微事件模拟框架，实现端到端优化；通过训练使滤波器自发演化为具有中心-周围结构的模式，突出中频成分。

Result: 所学空间滤波器自发形成类似人类CSF的中心-周围结构，有效增强中频信息；在目标检测和动作识别任务上取得显著性能提升，且对噪声具有强鲁棒性。

Conclusion: FS-DVS提供了一种生物合理、高效且通用的下一代类脑视觉传感新范式，其核心的中频选择性机制具有普适性，优于单纯提高灵敏度或依赖后处理的方法。

Abstract: Dynamic vision sensors (DVS) offer exceptional temporal resolution and dynamic range by asynchronously reporting pixel-level intensity changes. However, conventional DVS rely on a per-pixel independent triggering mechanism, ignoring the spatial integration performed by biological retinal ganglion cells (RGCs). Consequently, they lack the contrast sensitivity function (CSF) and its inherent sensitivity to mid-spatial frequencies, which inevitably leads to information incompleteness due to sub-threshold signal loss. To bridge this gap, we propose FS-DVS (Frequency-Selective Dynamic Vision Sensor), a novel paradigm that integrates a learnable spatial filter strictly preceding the event triggering process to mimic the RGC aggregation mechanism. By developing a differentiable event simulation framework, the spatial filter can be optimized end-to-end with downstream tasks. Our study reveals that starting from a delta function, the learned spatial filters spontaneously evolve into center-surround patterns that emphasize mid-frequency components, consistently aligning with human CSF. Beyond achieving substantial performance gains in object detection and action recognition, the consistent convergence to human-like CSF characteristics across different tasks underscores the universality of this mid-frequency selective mechanism. Compared to naively increasing sensor sensitivity or relying on post-processing, our paradigm achieves selective information enhancement with high noise resilience, providing a robust, biologically plausible blueprint for next-generation neuromorphic sensors.

### [25] [LRMIL: Efficient Low-Resolution Multiple Instance Learning via High-Resolution Knowledge Distillation for Whole Slide Image Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06864)
*Yonghan Shin,Won-Ki Jeong*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种高效的低分辨率多实例学习（LRMIL）框架，通过两阶段知识蒸馏策略将高分辨率知识迁移至低分辨率表示，从而在保持高性能的同时显著降低计算开销和数据预处理成本。该方法在多个全切片图像（WSI）基准上优于现有SOTA方法，具有临床应用的实用性和可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多实例学习（MIL）方法依赖于高分辨率图像块的密集提取与编码，在真实临床环境中存在两个关键问题：难以捕捉低倍率下的全局视觉线索，且因每张切片包含大量高分辨率块而导致巨大的计算开销。

Method: LRMIL采用两阶段知识蒸馏策略：第一阶段为块级跨分辨率蒸馏，对齐低分辨率块嵌入与高分辨率表示；第二阶段为切片级知识蒸馏，利用切片级监督与教师模型指导训练低分辨率学生MIL模型。推理时仅使用低分辨率块，大幅减少预处理与计算成本。

Result: 在多个全切片图像（WSI）基准上的实验表明，LRMIL在性能上持续优于现有最先进的MIL方法，同时实现更高效的推理，验证了其在临床病理分析中的实用性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: LRMIL是一种高效、可扩展的全切片图像分析解决方案，能够在低分辨率输入下实现高性能，显著降低计算负担，适合实际临床部署。

Abstract: Multiple instance learning (MIL) has become a standard paradigm for whole slide image (WSI) analysis in digital pathology, as it enables slide-level prediction without dense annotations. Existing MIL methods typically rely on exhaustive extraction and encoding of high-resolution patches. However, this practice suffers from two critical limitations in real-world clinical settings: it struggles to capture global visual cues at lower magnifications, and incurs substantial computational overhead due to the massive number of high-resolution patches per slide. To address these limitations, we propose an efficient low-resolution multiple instance learning (LRMIL) framework that transfers high-resolution knowledge to low-resolution representations. LRMIL adopts a two-stage distillation strategy. First, patch-level cross-resolution distillation aligns low-resolution patch embeddings with high-resolution representations. Second, slide-level knowledge distillation trains a low-resolution student MIL model under both slide-level supervision and teacher guidance. At inference time, LRMIL operates exclusively on low-resolution patches, substantially reducing data preprocessing and computational cost. Extensive experiments on multiple WSI benchmarks demonstrate that LRMIL consistently outperforms state-of-the-art MIL methods while achieving more efficient inference. These results highlight LRMIL as a practical and scalable solution for WSI analysis in clinical pathology.

Method: 提出Multi-FRuGaL框架，包含：1）各模态独立编码器；2）信号分解层以分离冗余与特定模态信号；3）输入条件门控网络，动态调整各模态贡献权重；4）信息感知融合目标，强化对关键信息的学习。整体设计支持模态缺失下的灵活融合与自适应加权。

Result: 在HANCOCK数据集上，Multi-FRuGaL将生存预测AUC从0.601提升至0.8496，复发预测从0.672提升至0.8102，并在进展/复发/总生存方面分别获得0.6814、0.7421、0.7143的C-index；在HECKTOR数据集上，HPV状态预测达到0.975 AUC，复发自由生存C-index达0.7203。在严重模态缺失情况下仍保持优异性能。

Conclusion: Multi-FRuGaL是一种高效、鲁棒且可扩展的多模态学习框架，能够在不完整数据条件下实现优越的性能，为临床决策支持系统中的多模态数据分析提供了强有力的技术支撑。

Abstract: Modern medicine relies on heterogeneous data sources spanning radiology, pathology, text reports, and structured clinical information. However, real-world patient data are frequently incomplete, with missing or sparsely acquired modalities, limiting the effectiveness of standard multimodal fusion approaches. To this end, we propose the Multimodal Flexible Redundancy-aware decomposed GAted Learning (Multi-FRuGaL) framework, a decomposition-aware, adaptive gated intermediate-fusion framework that performs modality-level representation learning under missing data. Multi-FRuGaL integrates per-modality encoders with a signal decomposition layer, an input-conditioned gating network, and an information-aware fusion objective to separate redundant from modality-specific complementary signals, selectively upweighting informative modalities and suppressing redundant or noisy inputs, and remaining well-defined even when multiple modalities are absent. We evaluate Multi-FRuGaL on two multimodal head and neck cancer cohorts: the HANCOCK challenge dataset (N = 763) comprising five modalities and two prognostic endpoints (5-year survival and 2-year recurrence), and the HECKTOR challenge dataset (N = 588) comprising three modalities for human papillomavirus (HPV) status classification. Multi-FRuGaL consistently achieves higher mean performance than the evaluated baselines across multiple tasks, improving AUC from 0.601 to 0.8496 for survival, from 0.672 to 0.8102 for recurrence, and achieving 0.975 AUC for HPV prediction on HECKTOR. For survival analysis, it further achieves a concordance index of 0.6814 for overall survival, 0.7421 for recurrence-free survival, and 0.7143 for progression-free survival on HANCOCK, and 0.7203 for recurrence-free survival on HECKTOR. Qualitative analyses further show that Multi-FRuGaL learns discriminative and robust multimodal representations, even under severe missing-modality conditions.

Existing methods often discretize pressure signal and process frames independently, leading to quantization errors and temporal inconsistencies. We present \emph{EgoPressDiff}, a conditional video diffusion framework that generates UV-pressure maps from visual input. The core of our approach is a multi-modal conditioning strategy, introducing a PoseNet and a Vertex Encoder to efficiently extract features from hand pose and 3D mesh vertices. These signals, along with depth information, guide the generative process to ensure the pressure fields are physically grounded. To effectively fuse these heterogeneous features, we further propose a Distribution-Calibrated Spatial Layer, which aligns their statistical properties before combination. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于多模态注意力的信息流分析，识别出不安全语义出现的启动阶段、任务相关的语义放大与干扰阶段，通过训练无关的注意力调制与有害信息流限制，实现对不安全内容的精准干预。

Conclusion: UVR是一种无需训练的统一安全调控框架，能够有效应对扩散变换器中图像生成与编辑任务中的不安全内容问题，具有良好的通用性和实用性。

Abstract: Diffusion transformers (DiTs) equipped with multimodal attention (MM-Attn) have become a dominant paradigm for image generation. However, preventing the generation of harmful content remains a critical challenge, particularly in image-to-image (I2I) editing tasks. Existing safety mechanisms are primarily designed for text-to-image (T2I) synthesis or U-Net-based architectures, which limits their effectiveness for unified safety mitigation in DiT-based frameworks. To bridge this gap, we propose Unified Visual Safety Regulator (UVR), a training-free safe generation framework that regulates unsafe semantics in generated images. UVR is grounded in an analysis of attention dynamics from the perspective of information flow in MM-Attn. We identify a task-independent start-up stage, during which unsafe semantics in output patches rapidly emerge and can be accurately localized, followed by task-specific semantic amplification and interference stages, where harmful signals are further propagated and entangled with benign content. Based on these observations, UVR mitigates unsafe generation through unified, targeted attention modulation and explicit restriction of harmful information flow over the identified unsafe output patches. Experiments across various concepts show that UVR achieves state-of-the-art safety performance by achieving 91% and 77% erase rate in image synthesis and editing tasks, while preserving visual quality and fidelity with minimal degradation. ### [29] [FreeAnimate: Training-Free Human Image Animation with Preview-Guided Denoising](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06885)
*Yuan Zeng,Yujia Shi,Zongqing Lu,QingMin Liao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: FreeAnimate 是一种无需训练的框架，利用图像扩散模型的内在能力实现时序一致性、身份保留和背景稳定。通过新颖的预览生成策略提供时序和结构先验，引导姿态对齐和背景一致性，并引入 Inversion-Boosted Attention 和 Reference-Anchored Self-Attention 模块以确保时序一致性和身份保留。实验表明，FreeAnimate 在生成质量上媲美最先进方法，且在不同数据集上表现出强泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于扩散模型的人像动画方法通常需要大量训练数据和资源，限制了其泛化能力和可及性。为解决这一问题，本文提出无需训练的 FreeAnimate 框架，旨在提升效率与通用性。

Method: 采用预览生成策略提供时序和结构先验，引导姿态对齐与背景一致性；引入 Inversion-Boosted Attention 和 Reference-Anchored Self-Attention 模块，以保障时序一致性和身份保留。

Result: FreeAnimate 在生成质量上优于现有无需训练的方法，达到与训练型基线相当的水平，具备优异的跨数据集泛化能力。

Conclusion: FreeAnimate 成功实现了无需训练的人像动画生成，在保证高质量输出的同时显著降低资源需求，具有良好的实用价值和推广潜力。

Abstract: Human Image Animation has seen significant advancements, primarily driven by diffusion models. However, existing methods typically demand substantial training data and resources to achieve high-quality results, limiting generalization and accessibility. In this work, we introduce \emph{FreeAnimate}, a training-free framework that leverages the inherent capabilities of image diffusion models to enable temporal consistency, identity preservation, and background stability. Our approach incorporates a novel preview generation strategy that provides temporal and structural priors from generated preview frames, effectively guiding pose alignment and background consistency without training. Additionally, FreeAnimate introduces Inversion-Boosted Attention and Reference-Anchored Self-Attention modules to guarantee temporal consistency and identity preservation. Experimental results demonstrate that FreeAnimate outperforms existing training-free competitors and training-based baseline methods, achieving generation quality comparable to state-of-the-art methods and offering robust generalization across diverse datasets. Our project page is at https://freeani.github.io/.

### [30] [ARAPDiffusion: ARAP Regularization for Diffusion-Based Deformable Shape Space Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06887)
*Haibo Liu,Jinghan Ke,Haitao Yang,Xiangru Huang,Georgios Pavlakos,Qixing Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ARAPDiffusion 是一种基于潜在扩散模型的形状生成方法，通过引入作为刚性尽可能（ARAP）的变形模型作为正则化损失，减少了对大量3D训练数据的需求。该方法在编码器/解码器和扩散模型之间交替优化，提升了形状重建与生成能力，并适用于无序点云。实验表明其在无条件与有条件生成任务中优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统生成模型依赖大量3D数据进行训练，而真实场景中高质量3D数据稀缺；同时，现有方法难以有效建模复杂形变空间。因此需要一种能利用少量数据并保持几何一致性与连续性的生成框架。

Method: 将ARAP变形模型嵌入潜空间扩散模型中，作为正则化项，在训练过程中交替优化编码器/解码器与扩散模型：一是用扩散模型生成的分布构建增强编码器/解码器的损失，二是用解码器输出构建优化扩散模型的损失。结合表示无关的扩散过程与隐式形状解码器，支持无序点云输入。

Result: 在无条件与条件形状生成任务中，ARAPDiffusion展现出更优的生成质量、几何保真度与多样性；相比基线方法，在少样本条件下仍具有较强泛化能力，且对无序点云具有良好的适用性。

Conclusion: ARAPDiffusion 通过融合ARAP正则化与潜空间扩散模型，成功学习了变形形状的连续潜空间，显著降低了对大规模3D数据的依赖，同时保持了高保真与灵活性，为低资源条件下的三维形状生成提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: This paper introduces ARAPDiffusion, a latent diffusion model to learn the underlying continuous shape space of a deformation shape collection. The key innovation is in injecting the as-rigid-as-possible (ARAP) deformation model as regularization losses into latent diffusion (LD), releasing the requirement of having abundant 3D training data for learning generative models. In contrast to the standard LD, we show how the ARAP model can be used to improve both the encoder/decoder and the LD model. The training procedure alternates between using the synthetic distribution defined by the LD model to develop a regularization loss that enhances the shape encoder/decoder and using the shape decoder to develop a regularization loss to improve the LD model. We also show the benefit of the LD paradigm in combining a representation-free LD process and an implicit shape decoder that is applicable to unorganized point clouds. The experimental results of unconditional and conditional shape generation demonstrate the advantages of ARAPDiffusion over baseline approaches.

### [31] [Diagnosing Visual Ignorance in Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06890)
*Runyu Zhou,Qi Zhang,Qixun Wang,Yisen Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究从机制和行为两个角度分析了视觉-语言模型（VLMs）对语言先验的依赖问题。通过反事实层替换与逐层MLP探测，发现模型内部存在多阶段瓶颈：中间层难以有效提取视觉信息，后期层则进一步抑制残存的视觉信号以迎合文本空间偏见。外部评估中引入渐进式视觉退化指标（基于多步高斯模糊），发现大量样本在严重甚至完全视觉遮蔽下仍能保持答案不变，表明当前基准测试可能无意中奖励对视觉信息的忽视。结果表明，语言先验依赖是一种系统性的信息路由失败，影响模型内部机制与评估有效性。最后提出未来研究方向：需设计基于结构隔离或反事实数据的训练分布与评估协议，以确保真正的跨模态对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前视觉-语言模型常依赖语言先验，产生看似自信但缺乏视觉证据支持的答案，这一现象虽被广泛观察，但其内在机制及对基准测试的影响尚不明确。亟需深入理解语言先验如何在模型内部传播并影响决策，以及现有评估方式是否合理反映真实跨模态理解能力。

Method: 结合反事实层替换与监督式逐层MLP探测，分析语言解码器中视觉语义与语言先验语义的竞争过程；引入基于多步高斯模糊的渐进式视觉退化指标，量化视觉信息破坏下答案的稳定性，从而识别模型是否真正依赖视觉输入。

Result: 揭示了模型内部存在多阶段信息路由瓶颈，后期层倾向于压制视觉信号；在十二个VQA基准和三个主流VLM上，大量样本在极端视觉退化下仍能正确回答，说明现有基准可能误判模型为具备跨模态理解能力，实则仅依赖语言先验。

Conclusion: 语言先验依赖是系统性路由失败的表现，既影响模型内部表征，也削弱现有评估基准的有效性。未来需构建基于反事实或结构隔离数据的训练与评估框架，以推动真正跨模态接地的模型发展。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) frequently rely on language priors, producing confident answers that are weakly grounded in visual evidence. While this behavior is widely observed, its internal mechanisms and its impact on benchmark evaluation remain insufficiently understood. In this work, we study language-prior reliance from both mechanistic and behavioral perspectives. Internally, we combine counterfactual layer replacement with supervised layer-wise MLP probing to trace how ground-truth visual semantics and language-prior semantics compete across the language decoder. Our analysis reveals a multi-stage bottleneck: intermediate layers often fail to effectively retrieve visual information, while later layers can further suppress surviving visual signals in favor of text-space biases. Externally, we introduce a progressive visual decay metric based on multi-step Gaussian blurring, which identifies instances whose answers remain invariant even as visual content is increasingly destroyed. Across twelve visual question-answering benchmarks and three representative VLMs, we find that a substantial fraction of examples remain answerable under severe or total visual obfuscation, indicating that current benchmarks can inadvertently reward visual ignorance. These findings demonstrate that language-prior reliance is a systematic routing failure affecting both model internals and benchmark validity. Finally, we outline critical pathways for future research, highlighting the necessity of designing training distributions and evaluation protocols built on structurally isolated or counterfactual data to enforce genuine cross-modal grounding.

While existing approaches typically address this issue through data augmentations that encourage models to become invariant to lighting changes, such strategies do not explicitly model lighting information during learning. Inspired by theories of human vision, we propose a lighting-aware representation learning framework that incorporates illumination variation as an explicit training signal rather than a nuisance factor to be suppressed. Our method extends contrastive learning by introducing an auxiliary objective that captures illumination-dependent variation in rendered scenes, enabling the model to jointly learn representations that preserve semantic consistency while remaining sensitive to lighting-dependent visual structure. These results indicate its potential to enhance model robustness and adaptability in complex visual environments as well as in more conventional image processing tasks.

### [34] [LUCID: Learning Unified Control for Image Deflaring and Exposure Mastery in Nighttime Photography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06901)
*Tingyu Yang,Yuan Cheng,Xiaoyun Yuan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LUCID 是一个统一的夜间图像修复框架，将夜间恢复视为连续可控的过程。它通过两个协同模块实现：去耀斑模块提供结构引导，扩散驱动模块利用生成先验重建清晰曝光的图像。引入四模式训练策略，支持通过无分类器指导（CFG）控制光照和耀斑/鬼影，以及通过连续曝光控制实现高动态范围（HDR）重建。在多种真实夜间场景中，LUCID 均显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法分别处理夜间图像中的耀斑和低光噪声问题，但忽略了二者本质上的耦合关系。为解决这一问题，需要一种能够统一建模并可控调节的修复框架。

Method: LUCID 采用双模块设计：1）耀斑解纠缠模块，去除光学伪影以提供可靠结构信息；2）扩散驱动模块，基于生成先验重建高质量图像。结合四模式训练策略与无分类器指导（CFG），实现对光照、耀斑、鬼影及曝光的精细控制。

Result: 在多种真实夜间场景下，LUCID 在视觉质量和定量指标上均超越当前最先进的方法，展现出更强的鲁棒性与可控性。

Conclusion: LUCID 成功将夜间图像修复从固定校正转向连续可控过程，实现了对复杂退化因素的有效分离与灵活调控，为高质量夜间成像提供了新范式。

Abstract: Photography is the art of painting with light, yet nighttime scenes are shaped by competing degradations: intense flares obscure scene structure, while photon-limited regions collapse into noise. Conventional approaches address these factors in isolation, overlooking the fact that these degradations are fundamentally entangled. To bridge this gap, we introduce LUCID, a unified framework that reframes nighttime restoration as a continuous and controllable process rather than a fixed correction. We decompose nighttime restoration into two cooperative components: a flare disentanglement module that lifts the 'curtain' of optical artifacts to provide reliable structural guidance, and a diffusion-driven module that leverages generative priors to reconstruct clean and well-exposed imagery. Crucially, LUCID introduces explicit controllability through a novel four-mode training strategy, enabling users to steer the restoration process via classifier-free guidance (CFG) and allowing selective control over light sources and their associated flare and ghosting artifacts, while also supporting high dynamic range (HDR) reconstruction through continuous exposure control. Extensive experiments demonstrate that LUCID consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods across diverse real-world nighttime scenarios.

### [35] [Beyond Skeletons: Learning Animation Directly from Driving Videos with Same2X Training Strategy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06903)

Abstract: Human image animation aims to generate a video from a static reference image, guided by pose information extracted from a driving video. Existing approaches often rely on pose estimators to extract intermediate representations, but such signals are prone to errors under occlusion or complex poses. Building on these observations, we present DirectAnimator, a framework that bypasses pose extraction and directly learns from raw driving videos. We introduce a Driving Cue Triplet consisting of pose, face, and location cues that captures motion, expression, and alignment in a semantically rich yet stable form, and we fuse them through a CueFusion DiT block for reliable control during denoising. To make learning dependable when the driving and reference identities differ, we devise a Same2X training strategy that aligns cross-ID features with those learned from same-ID data, regularizing optimization and accelerating convergence. ### [36] [polyDAG: Polynomial Acyclicity Constraints for Efficient Continuous Causal Discovery in Visual Semantic Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06908)
*Wenhao Zhang,Ramin Ramezani,Tao Han,Kai Hwang,Minyi Guo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出polyDAG，一种基于多项式迹约束的高效连续因果发现框架，用于视觉语义图中的无环图学习。通过替代矩阵指数约束为多项式迹约束，证明其在无环图上精确为零，并引入几何级数实现避免显式求和循环，保持相同无环条件。在合成Erdos-Renyi图和CelebA人脸属性数据上的实验表明，该方法在结构恢复和效率方面均优于基线，平均结构汉明距离从318.4降至285.4，F1分数从0.725提升至0.756，在100节点下速度提升33.4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有连续有向无环图（DAG）学习方法受限于强制无环性带来的高昂计算成本，尤其在大规模视觉语义图中。因此需要更高效的无环性约束机制以支持可扩展的因果发现。

Method: 提出polyDAG框架，用有限多项式迹约束替代传统的矩阵指数无环性约束，并设计几何级数形式实现，避免显式求和，同时保证无环性等价条件。

Result: 在合成图与CelebA数据集上，polyDAG显著提升结构恢复精度（降低平均结构汉明距离、提高F1分数），并在100节点时实现33.4%的速度提升，整体效率与准确性均优于基线方法。

Conclusion: polyDAG通过多项式迹约束与几何级数实现，实现了高效且准确的连续因果发现，适用于大规模视觉语义图建模，具有良好的可扩展性和实用性。

Abstract: Modern image-analysis pipelines often convert images into structured semantic variables, such as facial attributes, object concepts, and scene descriptors. Learning directed dependencies among these variables can produce interpretable visual semantic graphs, but continuous directed acyclic graph learning is limited by the cost of enforcing acyclicity. We present polyDAG, a polynomial acyclicity framework for efficient continuous causal discovery in visual semantic graphs. polyDAG replaces the matrix-exponential acyclicity constraint with a finite polynomial trace constraint and proves that the new constraint is zero exactly for acyclic graphs. We further derive a geometric-series implementation that avoids the explicit summation loop while preserving the same acyclicity condition. Experiments on synthetic Erdos-Renyi graphs and CelebA facial visual attributes show that polyDAG improves efficiency and structure recovery. Averaged over the revised synthetic protocol with d in {100, 200, 500}, polyDAG reduces mean structural Hamming distance from 318.4 to 285.4 and improves mean F1 score from 0.725 to 0.756. At 100 nodes, the geometric variant runs in 3.44 seconds compared with 5.16 seconds for the exponential baseline, corresponding to a 33.4 percent speedup. Code and data are publicly available at https://github.com/wenhaoz-fengcai/polyDAG.

</details>


### [37] [DRIFT: From Robustness Gaps to Invariance Manifolds for AI-Generated Image Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06918)
*Abhishek Ameta,Sayan Banerjee,Shreyas Pandith,Harshit,Ankita Chatterjee,Akshay Janardan Bankar,Amit Satish Unde*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的AI生成图像检测方法，通过在冻结的视觉基础模型（VFM）上引入轻量级投影头，将表示空间分解为鲁棒和脆弱子空间。鲁棒子空间抑制物理合理成像变换引起的差异，逼近真实图像流形的切线方向；脆弱子空间保留对编辑类扰动的敏感性。通过结构化排序边界强制两者之间的层次分离，实现基于流形偏差的检测。推理时采用多尺度块级漂移分析，生成双通道不变性签名与可解释的定位图，在未见生成器和分辨率下表现出优异的开放世界泛化能力，优于现有训练无关基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有训练无关方法依赖预训练中固有的不变性几何，缺乏针对检测任务的合理适应，难以应对开放世界中新出现的生成模型。需要一种能动态学习真实图像不变性流形并有效区分物理变换与编辑扰动的方法。

Method: 在冻结的视觉基础模型基础上，设计轻量级投影头以分解表示空间为鲁棒与脆弱子空间；鲁棒子空间通过对抗训练抑制物理成像变换的影响，逼近真实图像流形的切线方向；脆弱子空间保持对编辑类扰动的敏感性；利用结构化排序边界实现两者的层级分离，并以边际违反测试作为检测依据；推理阶段采用多尺度块级漂移分析，生成双通道不变性签名与可解释的异常定位图。

Result: 在多种未见过的生成器和分辨率设置下均表现出强开放世界泛化性能，显著优于现有训练无关方法，同时提供可解释的不变性违反地图，支持精准定位伪造区域。

Conclusion: 本文提出的方法通过学习结构化的不变性流形，实现了对生成图像的有效检测，兼具高精度、强泛化性和可解释性，为开放世界场景下的深度伪造检测提供了新范式。

Abstract: The rapid evolution of generative image models challenges existing AI-generated image detectors, particularly in open-world settings with unseen generators. Recent training-free approaches measure robustness gaps in frozen vision foundation models (VFMs), detecting fakes via perturbation-induced embedding drift. However, these methods rely on fixed invariance geometry inherited from pretraining and lack principled adaptation to the detection task. We instead formulate AI-generated image detection as learning a structured invariance manifold of real images under one-class supervision. Building upon a frozen VFM, we introduce lightweight projection heads that decompose representation space into complementary robust and fragile subspaces. The robust subspace is explicitly trained to suppress variations induced by physically plausible imaging transformations, approximating tangent directions of a real-image manifold, while the fragile subspace retains sensitivity to edit-like perturbations. A structured ordering margin enforces hierarchical separation between physical invariance and edit-induced variability, enabling detection as a margin-violation test relative to the learned manifold. At inference, multi-scale patch-wise drift under both transformation families yields a dual-channel invariance signature and interpretable localization. Extensive experiments demonstrate strong open-world generalization across unseen generators and resolutions, consistently outperforming training-free robustness-based baselines while providing interpretable invariance-violation maps.

### [38] [SVHighlights: Towards Extremely Long Sport Video Highlight Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06926)
*Donggyu Lee,Youngbin Ki,Jeonghun Kang,Taehwan Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了SVHighlights，首个针对超长体育视频（每段超过一小时）的亮点检测基准，涵盖320个视频，总时长达640.18小时。为解决现有方法在长视频上表现不佳的问题，提出无需训练的TF-SELECTOR方法，通过语义一致的镜头合并生成上下文感知片段，并利用多模态大语言模型（视觉描述、字幕、音频音量）预测片段级显著性得分。实验表明，TF-SELECTOR在多项指标上优于基于VTG微调的基线，显著提升在HIT@1、HIT@K和IoU上的表现，验证了该基准的挑战性及段落级策略在长视频中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有亮点检测方法主要针对短时视频，缺乏适用于超长体育视频的基准数据集，且传统方法在长视频中因缺乏全局上下文而难以泛化，亟需新的评估标准与有效方法。

Method: 提出SVHighlights基准，基于全视频与官方剪辑配对生成标签；设计TF-SELECTOR方法，将视频按语义内容合并相邻镜头形成上下文感知片段，并使用多模态大语言模型（视觉描述、字幕、音频音量）预测片段显著性得分，实现无需训练的端到端亮点检测。

Conclusion: SVHighlights是首个面向超长体育视频的亮点检测基准，填补了该领域的空白；提出的TF-SELECTOR方法虽无训练过程，却能有效捕捉长视频中的全局语义信息，展现出强大的可扩展性与性能优势，为未来研究提供了坚实基础。

Abstract: While highlight detection for long-form videos is of great practical importance, most existing methods remain limited to short-form content, largely due to the absence of a suitable benchmark. To bridge this gap, we introduce SVHighlights, to the best of our knowledge, the first benchmark for highlight detection in extremely long sports videos, each exceeding one hour in duration, across multiple sports categories. SVHighlights is constructed from pairs of full-length sports videos and their corresponding official highlight videos using a dataset generation pipeline, enabling scalable label generation without conventional per-clip saliency annotation. The benchmark comprises 320 videos with an average duration of 2.00 hours and a total of 640.18 hours, substantially exceeding previous datasets. Existing methods also face fundamental challenges on long videos: models trained on short clips fail to generalize to hour-long content, and their clip-level scoring lacks the broader context needed to identify highlights. To address this and provide a strong baseline, we present TF-SELECTOR, a training-free segment-based approach that divides each video into context-aware segments by merging adjacent shots sharing the same semantic content, and predicts segment-level saliency scores using a large language model with multimodal inputs including visual captions, transcripts, and audio volume. Experiments demonstrate that TF-SELECTOR achieves superior performance across most metrics compared to Video Temporal Grounding (VTG)-tuned baselines, with improvements of +3.12 in HIT@1, +4.06 in HIT@K, and +2.95 in IoU. These results establish SVHighlights as a challenging testbed for long-form highlight detection and demonstrate that a simple segment-based strategy can effectively scale to hour-long videos.

### [39] [When CLIP Sees More, It Fights Back Harder: Multi-View Guided Adaptive Counterattacks for Test-Time Adversarial Robustness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06938)
*Sunoh Kim,Daeho Um*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为多视图引导自适应对抗攻击（MAC）的新方法，用于提升CLIP等视觉-语言模型在面对对抗性扰动时的鲁棒性。MAC通过构建输入图像的多个增强视图，生成多样化嵌入，并针对每个视图进行自适应强度的对抗攻击以修复受损嵌入。该方法根据各视图的估计污染程度动态调整对抗攻击强度，再将自适应修正后的视图聚合得到最终预测结果。实验表明，MAC在20个数据集和多种攻击场景下显著提升了鲁棒性，同时保持了高推理速度和内存效率，且无需调参。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试时对抗攻击（TTC）方法对强攻击仍显脆弱，因其依赖直接损坏的原始视图，并采用无法适应不同污染严重程度的噪声驱动硬门控策略，限制了其鲁棒性提升效果。

Method: MAC首先生成输入图像的多视图增强表示，获取多样化的嵌入；随后对各视图的受损嵌入执行对抗攻击进行修复；接着基于各视图的污染程度估计，自适应地调节对抗攻击强度；最后融合所有经过自适应修正的视图，输出鲁棒的最终预测结果。

Result: 在20个不同数据集和多种攻击场景下的大量实验验证了MAC的有效性：相比现有方法，MAC在对抗鲁棒性上实现显著提升，同时保持了高速推理与低内存开销，且设计为无需调参。

Conclusion: MAC通过多视图引导与污染感知的自适应软加权机制，有效克服了传统TTC方法在强攻击下的局限性，是提升视觉-语言模型对抗鲁棒性的高效、轻量级方案。

Abstract: Vision-language models such as CLIP have achieved remarkable zero-shot recognition capabilities, yet their robustness against adversarial perturbations remains limited. Test-time counterattack (TTC) was recently proposed to improve CLIP's robustness by perturbing an input image to steer it away from a corrupted state during inference. However, TTC remains fragile under strong attacks because its counterattack relies on a directly corrupted original view and employs a noise-driven hard-gating scheme that cannot adapt to varying corruption severity. To address these limitations, we introduce Multi-view guided Adaptive Counterattack (MAC), which performs counterattacks for multi-view with corruption-aware soft weighting. Specifically, MAC first constructs augmented views of an input image to obtain diverse embeddings. It then performs counterattacks to refine corrupted embeddings of views. Next, MAC adaptively scales the counterattack intensity for each view based on its estimated corruption degree. Finally, the adaptively counterattacked views are aggregated to yield a robust final prediction. Extensive experiments across 20 datasets and diverse attack scenarios demonstrate that MAC substantially improves robustness while preserving high inference speed and memory efficiency with its tuning-free design. Our code is available at https://github.com/sunoh-kim/MAC.

</details>


### [40] [SS-TPT: Stability and Suitability-Guided Test-Time Prompt Tuning for Adversarially Robust Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06943)
*Sunoh Kim,Daeho Um*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出SS-TPT方法，通过稳定性（stability）和适用性（suitability）双重评分机制，在测试时自适应地筛选增强视图，提升视觉语言模型在对抗扰动下的鲁棒性，同时实现高效推理，显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试时自适应防御方法依赖大量增强视图，导致计算开销大、吞吐率下降，存在鲁棒性与效率的权衡问题。

Method: 设计稳定性与适用性双评分机制：稳定性衡量弱增强下预测的一致性，适用性衡量视图间特征空间密度；利用该评分构建一致性损失与加权预测策略，强化可信视图，抑制受损视图。

Result: 在多个数据集上，SS-TPT显著优于当前最先进方法，实现了更优的鲁棒性-吞吐率平衡，兼具实用性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: SS-TPT通过双评分机制有效提升了视觉语言模型在对抗攻击下的鲁棒性，同时保持高推理效率，是一种高效且通用的测试时自适应防御方案。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) such as CLIP achieve strong zero-shot recognition but remain highly fragile under adversarial perturbations. Recent test-time adaptation defenses improve robustness by leveraging many augmented views, but this leads to impractical slowdown and a clear robustness-throughput trade-off. To address this challenge, we present Stability and Suitability-guided Test-time Prompt Tuning (SS-TPT), evaluating the quality of each augmented view via two complementary scores: (1) stability, measuring prediction invariance to weak augmentations, and (2) suitability, measuring feature-space density among views. These stability and suitability (SS) scores guide both adaptation and inference through an SS-guided consistency loss and an SS-weighted prediction, amplifying trustworthy views while suppressing corrupted ones. Extensive experiments demonstrate that SS-TPT significantly outperforms prior state-of-the-art methods, achieving superior robustness-throughput trade-offs across diverse datasets and varying numbers of views, thereby demonstrating both strong practicality and generality. Our code is available at https://github.com/sunoh-kim/SS-TPT.

</details>


### [41] [When is 3D Worth It? A Resource-Performance Frontier for CNNs and Transformers in Lung CT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06950)
*Md Enamul Hoq,Sharafat Hossain,Imraul Emmaka,Linda Larson-Prior,Lawrence Tarbox,Jonathan Bona,Donald Johann Jr. and Fred Prior*
